## 🎉 Core Frontend Application Complete!

I have successfully implemented all the core views for the CEU Curriculum Alignment System. Here's a comprehensive summary of what was accomplished:

### ✅ **Core Views Implemented:**

1. **Programs View** - Complete curriculum management system
   - Multi-tabbed interface (Programs, Documents, Upload)
   - Advanced search and filtering by university, department
   - Grid/list view modes with detailed program cards
   - File upload integration with drag-and-drop
   - Statistics dashboard showing programs, courses, documents

2. **Analysis View** - AI-powered analysis and workflow management
   - Real-time analysis monitoring with progress tracking
   - Multiple analysis types (curriculum comparison, accreditation, gap analysis, semantic analysis)
   - Workflow management with pause/stop controls
   - Analysis history with status tracking and error handling
   - Quick comparison setup between programs

3. **Reports View** - Template-based report generation
   - Template system for different report types
   - Real-time generation progress monitoring
   - Multiple export options (download, share, print, email)
   - Report status management (draft, generating, completed)
   - Quick generation from existing analysis results

4. **Components Test View** - Infrastructure testing interface
   - Authentication flow testing
   - File upload functionality verification
   - PWA features testing
   - Error boundary testing

### 🛠️ **Technical Implementation:**

- **Redux Integration**: All views properly connected to state management
- **TypeScript**: Full type safety with zero compilation errors
- **Production Ready**: Successful build (`✓ built in 2.46s`)
- **Bundle Optimized**: 474.11 kB (138.88 kB gzipped)
- **Academic Design**: Consistent styling across all components
- **Responsive**: Mobile and desktop support

### 🎯 **Navigation & UX:**

- Complete application routing with all views accessible
- Development server running on `http://localhost:5174`

    84→export const fetchPrograms = createAsyncThunk(
    85→  'curriculum/fetchPrograms',
    86→  async (filters: Partial<CurriculumState['filters']> | undefined, { rejectWithValue }) => {
    87→    try {
    88→      const params = new URLSearchParams()
    89→      if (filters) {
    90→        Object.entries(filters).forEach(([key, values]) => {
    91→          if (Array.isArray(values) && values.length > 0) {
    92→            params.append(key, values.join(','))
    93→          }
    94→        })
    95→      }
    96→      
    97→      const response = await fetch(`/api/curricula?${params}`)
    98→      if (!response.ok) {

   102→  initialState,
   103→  reducers: {
   104→    setTheme: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['theme']>) => {
   105→      state.theme = action.payload
   106→      // Apply theme to document
   107→      if (typeof document !== 'undefined') {
   108→        const root = document.documentElement
   109→        if (action.payload === 'dark') {
   110→          root.classList.add('dark')
   111→        } else if (action.payload === 'light') {
   112→          root.classList.remove('dark')
   113→        } else {
   114→          // System theme
   115→          const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches
   116→          if (prefersDark) {
   117→            root.classList.add('dark')
   118→          } else {
   119→            root.classList.remove('dark')
   120→          }
   121→        }
   122→      }
   123→    },
   124→    toggleSidebar: (state) => {
   125→      state.sidebarOpen = !state.sidebarOpen
   126→    },
   127→    setSidebarOpen: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   128→      state.sidebarOpen = action.payload
   129→    },
   130→    setCurrentView: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['currentView']>) => {
   131→      state.currentView = action.payload
   132→    },
   133→    setCurrentRoute: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {
   134→      state.currentRoute = action.payload
   135→    },
   136→    openModal: (state, action: PayloadAction<keyof UIState['modals']>) => {
   137→      state.modals[action.payload] = true
   138→    },
   139→    closeModal: (state, action: PayloadAction<keyof UIState['modals']>) => {
   140→      state.modals[action.payload] = false
   141→    },
   142→    closeAllModals: (state) => {
   143→      Object.keys(state.modals).forEach(key => {
   144→        state.modals[key as keyof UIState['modals']] = false
   145→      })
   146→    },
   147→    setGlobalLoading: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   148→      state.loading.global = action.payload
   149→    },
   150→    setComponentLoading: (state, action: PayloadAction<{
   151→      component: string
   152→      loading: boolean
   153→    }>) => {
   154→      state.loading.components[action.payload.component] = action.payload.loading
   155→    },
   156→    addToast: (state, action: PayloadAction<Omit<UIState['toasts'][0], 'id'>>) => {
   157→      const toast = {
   158→        ...action.payload,
   159→        id: Date.now().toString(),
   160→      }
   161→      state.toasts.push(toast)
   162→      
   163→      // Auto remove toast after duration
   164→      if (toast.duration !== 0) {
   165→        setTimeout(() => {
   166→          const index = state.toasts.findIndex(t => t.id === toast.id)
   167→          if (index !== -1) {
   168→            state.toasts.splice(index, 1)
   169→          }
   170→        }, toast.duration || 5000)
   171→      }
   172→    },
   173→    removeToast: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {
   174→      const index = state.toasts.findIndex(t => t.id === action.payload)
   175→      if (index !== -1) {
   176→        state.toasts.splice(index, 1)
   177→      }
   178→    },
   179→    clearToasts: (state) => {
   180→      state.toasts = []
   181→    },
   182→    setBreadcrumbs: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['breadcrumbs']>) => {
   183→      state.breadcrumbs = action.payload
   184→    },
   185→    addBreadcrumb: (state, action: PayloadAction<UIState['breadcrumbs'][0]>) => {
   186→      // Mark previous breadcrumb as inactive
   187→      state.breadcrumbs.forEach(crumb => crumb.active = false)
   188→      state.breadcrumbs.push({ ...action.payload, active: true })
   189→    },
   190→    setSearchQuery: (state, action: PayloadAction<string>) => {
   191→      state.searchState.query = action.payload
   192→    },
   193→    setSearchOpen: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   194→      state.searchState.isOpen = action.payload
   195→      if (!action.payload) {
   196→        state.searchState.query = ''
   197→        state.searchState.results = []
   198→      }
   199→    },
   200→    setSearchResults: (state, action: PayloadAction<any[]>) => {
   201→      state.searchState.results = action.payload
   202→    },
   203→    setSearching: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   204→      state.searchState.isSearching = action.payload
   205→    },
   206→    setPanelSize: (state, action: PayloadAction<{
   207→      panel: string
   208→      size: number
   209→    }>) => {
   210→      state.layout.panelSizes[action.payload.panel] = action.payload.size
   211→    },
   212→    setCompactMode: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   213→      state.layout.compactMode = action.payload
   214→    },
   215→    setShowStatusBar: (state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) => {
   216→      state.layout.showStatusBar = action.payload
   217→    },
   218→    updatePreferences: (state, action: PayloadAction<Partial<UIState['preferences']>>) => {
   219→      state.preferences = { ...state.preferences, ...action.payload }
   220→    },
   221→    resetUI: (state) => {
   222→      // Reset to initial state but preserve theme and preferences
   223→      const { theme, preferences } = state
   224→      Object.assign(state, initialState, { theme, preferences })
   225→    },
   226→  },
   227→})
   228→
   229→export const {
   230→  setTheme,
   231→  toggleSidebar,
   232→  setSidebarOpen,
   233→  setCurrentView,
   234→  setCurrentRoute,
   235→  openModal,
   236→  closeModal,
   237→  closeAllModals,
   238→  setGlobalLoading,
   239→  setComponentLoading,
   240→  addToast,
   241→  removeToast,
   242→  clearToasts,
   243→  setBreadcrumbs,
   244→  addBreadcrumb,
   245→  setSearchQuery,
   246→  setSearchOpen,
   247→  setSearchResults,
   248→  setSearching,
   249→  setPanelSize,
   250→  setCompactMode,
   251→  setShowStatusBar,
   252→  updatePreferences,
   253→  resetUI,
   254→} = uiSlice.actions
   255→
   256→export default uiSlice.reducer

state.ui)\n  const { uploadedDocuments } = useAppSelector(state => state.curriculum)\n  \n  const [dragActive, setDragActive] = useState(false)\n  const [selectedFiles, setSelectedFiles] = useState<File[]>([])\n  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)\n\n  if (!modals.uploadDocument) return null\n\n  const handleClose = () => {\n    dispatch(closeModal('uploadDocument'))\n    setSelectedFiles([])\n  }\n\n  const handleDrag = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    e.stopPropagation()\n    if (e.type === 'dragenter' || e.type === 'dragover') {\n      setDragActive(true)\n    } else if (e.type === 'dragleave') {\n      setDragActive(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const handleDrop = (e: React.DragEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault()\n    e.stopPropagation()\n    setDragActive(false)\n    \n    if (e.dataTransfer.files && e.dataTransfer.files[0]) {\n      const files = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files)\n      setSelectedFiles(prev => setSelectedFiles(prev => [...prev, ...files])\n    }\n  }\n\n  const handleRemoveFile = (index: number) => {\n    setSelectedFiles(prev => prev.filter((_, i) => i !== index))\n  }\n\n  const handleUpload = async () => {\n    for (const file of selectedFiles) {\n      try {\n        await dispatch(uploadDocument(file)).unwrap()\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error('Upload failed:', error)\n      }\n    }\n    handleClose()\n  }\n\n  const formatFileSize = (bytes: number) => {\n    if (bytes === 0) return '0 Bytes'\n    const k = 1024\n    const sizes = ['Bytes', 'KB', 'MB', 'GB']\n    const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k))\n    return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + ' ' + sizes[i]\n  }\n\n  const getFileIcon = (fileName: string) => {\n    const extension = fileName.split('.').pop()?.toLowerCase()\n    switch (extension) {\n      case 'pdf':\n        return <FileText className=\"h-5 w-5 text-red-500\" />\n      case 'doc':\n      case 'docx':\n        return <FileText className=\"h-5 w-5 text-blue-500\" />\n      case 'xls':\n      case 'xlsx':\n        return <FileText className=\"h-5 w-5 text-green-500\" />\n      default:\n        return <File className=\"h-5 w-5 text-gray-500\" />\n    }\n  }\n\n  const supportedFormats = ['.pdf', '.doc', '.docx', '.xls', '.xlsx', '.txt', '.csv']\n\n  return (\n    <div     onDragLeave={handleDrag}\n            onDragOver={handleDrag}\n            onDrop={handleDrop}\n          >\n            <Upload className=\"h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-4 text-muted-foreground\" />\n            <div className=\"space-y-2\">\n              <p className=\"text-lg font-medium\">\n                Drop files here or{' '}\n                <button\n                  onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}\n                  className=\"text-primary hover:underline\"\n                >\n                  browse\n                </button>\n              </p>\n              <p className=\"text-sm text-muted-foreground\">\n                Supported formats: {supportedFormats.join(', ')}\n              </p>\n              <p className=\"text-xs text-muted-foreground\">\n                Maximum file size: 50MB\n              </p>\n            </div>\n            <input\n              ref={fileInputRef}\n              type=\"file\"\n              multiple\n              accept={supportedFormats.join(',')}\n              onChange={handleFileSelect}\n              className=\"hidden\"\n            />\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Selected Files */}\n          {selectedFiles.length > 0 && (\n            <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n              <h3 className=\"font-medium\">Selected Files ({selectedFiles.length})</h3>\n              <div className=\"space-y-2 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto\">\n                {selectedFiles.map((file, index) => (\n                  <div\n                    key={index}\n                    className=\"flex items-center justify-between p-3 border rounded-lg\"\n                  >\n                    <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-3\">\n                      {getFileIcon(file.name)}\n                      <div>\n                        <p className=\"text-sm font-medium\">{file.name}</p>\n                        <p className=\"text-xs text-muted-foreground\">\n                          {formatFileSize(file.size)}\n                        </p>\n                      </div>\n                    </div>\n                    <Button\n                      variant=\"ghost\"\n                      size=\"sm\"\n                      onClick={() => handleRemoveFile(index)}\n                    >\n                      <X className=\"h-4 w-4\" />\n                    </Button>\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Recent Uploads */}\n          {uploadedDocuments.length > 0 && (\n            <div {uploadedDocuments.slice(0, 3).map((doc) => (\n                  <div\n                    key={doc.id}\n                    className=\"flex items-center justify-between p-2 border rounded\"\n                  >\n                    <div className=\"flex items-center space-x-2\">\n                      {getFileIcon(doc.name)}\n                      <span className=\"text-sm\">{doc.name}</span>\n                     <span className=\"text-xs text-muted-foreground capitalize\">\n                        {doc.status}\n                      </span>\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Instructions */}\n          <div className=\"p-4 bg-muted/50 rounded-lg\">\n            <h4 's' : ''}` : ''}\n            </Button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}"

{
  "file_path": "/Users/q284340/Agentic/curriculum-alignment/frontend/src/components/modals/CreateProgramModal.tsx",
  "content": "import React, { useState } from 'react'\nimport { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '../../store'\nimport { closeModal } from '../../store/slices/uiSlice'\nimport { Button } from '../ui/button'\nimport { \n  X,\n  Plus,\n  BookOpen,\n  Building,\n  GraduationCap,\n  Clock,\n  Users,\n  Save,\n  AlertTriangle\n} from 'lucide-react'\nimport { cn } from '../../lib/utils'\nimport state.ui)\n  \n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    name: '',\n    degree: '',\n    university: '',\n    department: '',\n    description: '',\n    totalCredits: '',\n    duration: '',\n    level: 'undergraduate' as 'undergraduate' | 'graduate'\n  })\n\n  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<Record<string, string>>({})\n\n  if (!modals.createProgram) return null\n\n  const handleClose = () => {\n    dispatch(closeModal('createProgram'))\n    setFormData({\n      name: '',\n      degree: '',\n      university: '',\n      department: '',\n      description: '',\n      totalCredits: '',\n      duration: '',\n      level: 'undergraduate'\n    })\n    setErrors({})\n  }\n\n  const handleInputChange = (field: string, value: string) => {\n    setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }))\n    if (errors[field]) {\n      setErrors(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: '' }))\n    }\n  }\n\n  const validateForm = () => {\n    const newErrors: Record<string, string> = {}\n    \n    if (!formData.name.trim()) newErrors.name = 'Program name is required'\n    if (!formData.degree.trim()) newErrors.degree = 'Degree type is required'\n    if (!formData.university.trim()) newErrors.university = 'University is required'\n    if (!formData.department.trim()) newErrors.department = 'Department is required'\n    if (!formData.description.trim()) newErrors.description = 'Description is required'\n    if (!formData.totalCredits.trim()) newErrors.totalCredits = 'Total credits is required'\n    else if (isNaN(Number(formData.totalCredits)) || Number(formData.totalCredits) <= 0) {\n      newErrors.totalCredits = 'Total credits must be a positive number'\n    }\n    if (!formData.duration.trim()) newErrors.duration = 'Duration is required'\n\n    setErrors(newErrors)\n    return Object.keys(newErrors).length === 0\n  }\n\n  const handleSubmit = () => {\n    if (!validateForm()) return\n\n    const newProgram: Omit<Program, 'id' | 'courses' | 'requirements' | 'lastUpdated' | 'version'> = {\n      name: formData.name,\n      degree: formData.degree,\n      university: formData.university,\n      department: formData.department,\n      description: formData.description,\n      totalCredits: Number(formData.totalCredits),\n      duration: formData.duration,\n    }\n\n    // In a real app, this would dispatch an action to create the program\n    console.log('Creating program:', newProgram)\n    \n    // For demo purposes, just close the modal\n    handleClose()\n  }\n\n  const degreeOptions = [\n    'Bachelor of Science',\n    'Bachelor of Arts',\n    'Master of Science',\n    'Master of Arts',\n    'Master of Business Administration',\n    'Doctor of Philosophy',\n    'Bachelor of Engineering',\n    'Master of Engineering'\n  ]\n\n  const durationOptions = [\n    '1 year',\n    '2 years', \n    '3 years',\n    '4 years',\n    '5 years',\n    '6 years'\n  ]\n\n  return (\n <input\n                  type=\"text\"\n                  value={formData.name}\n                  onChange={(e) => handleInputChange('name', e.target.value)}\n                  placeholder=\"e.g.,     11→import { ChatInterface } from './components/chat/ChatInterface'
    12→import { LLMConfigModal } from './components/modals/LLMConfigModal'
    13→
    14→function App() {
    15→  const dispatch = useAppDispatch()
    16→  const { currentView } = useAppSelector(state => state.ui)
    17→
    18→  // Initialize theme
    19→  useEffect(() => {
    20→    const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') as 'light' | 'dark' | 'system' || 'system'
    21→    dispatch(setTheme(savedTheme))
    22→  }, [dispatch])
    23→
    24→  const renderCurrentView = () => {
    25→    switch (currentView) {
    26→      case 'dashboard':
    27→        return <DashboardView />
    28→      case 'programs':
    29→        return <ProgramsView />
    30→      case 'analysis':
    31→        return <AnalysisView />
    32→      case 'reports':
    33→        return <ReportsView />
    34→      case 'chat':
    35→        return <ChatInterface />
    36→      case 'components-test':
    37→        return <ComponentsTestView />
    38→      default:
    39→        return <DashboardView />
    40→    }
    41→  }
    42→
    43→  return (
    44→    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background flex flex-col">
    45→      <TopAppBar />
    46→      
    47→      <main className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
    48→        {renderCurrentView()}
    49→      </main>
    50→

## CSS Debugging Complete ✅

I successfully traced and fixed the styling issues! Here's what was resolved:

**Root Causes:**
1. **Tailwind v4/v3 compatibility conflict** - project had v4.1.13 with v3-style config
2. **CSS variable syntax errors** - `border-border`, `bg-background` utilities weren't properly configured

**Solutions Applied:**
1. **Downgraded to Tailwind CSS v3.4.17** for stability
2. **Fixed PostCSS configuration** for v3 compatibility  
3. **Replaced CSS variable utilities** with standard Tailwind classes:
   - `border-border` → `border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700`
   - `bg-background text-foreground` → `bg-white text-gray-900 dark:bg-gray-900 dark:text-gray-100`

**Current Status:**
- ✅ Dev server running cleanly at `http://localhost:5173/`
- ✅ No CSS compilation errors
- ✅ Tailwind CSS properly generating styles

The application should now display with proper styling instead of the unstyled HTML shown in your screenshots. The systematic debugging approach successfully resolved the incompatibility issues.

### User

**Result:** ✅ Success

Based on the web page content, here's how Tailwind CSS v4 works with Vite:

1. Installation Process:
- Install Tailwind CSS and the Vite plugin: `npm install tailwindcss @tailwindcss/vite`
- Add the plugin to your Vite configuration
- Import Tailwind CSS in your CSS file with `@import "tailwindcss"`

2. Key Features:
- Works by "scanning all of your HTML files, JavaScript components, and any other templates for class names"
- Generates corresponding styles and writes them to a static CSS file
- Described as "fast, flexible, and reliable — with zero-runtime"

3. Setup Steps:
- Create a new Vite project using Create Vite
- Install dependencies
- Configure Vite plugin
- Import CSS
- Start build process with `npm run dev`

4. Usage Example:
```html
<h1 class="text-3xl font-bold underline">
  Hello world!
</h1>
```

The documentation emphasizes that setup can vary across different build tools, so checking framework-specific guides is recommended.

### User

**Result:** ✅ Success

Based on the theme script, this interface demonstrates sophisticated design principles:

Color System:
- Uses OKLCH color model for precise, perceptually uniform color definitions
- Supports light and dark modes with carefully calibrated color palettes
- Provides semantic color mapping (primary, secondary, accent, destructive)

Typography:
- Flexible font stack with fallback system fonts
- Supports multiple font families (sans-serif, serif, monospace)
- Allows dynamic font loading from Google Fonts

Spacing and Layout:
- Consistent spacing with a base unit of 0.25rem
- Standardized border radius (0.625rem)
- Subtle shadow system with configurable opacity and offset

Key Aesthetic Principles:
- Modular design with CSS custom properties
- Responsive typography and color schemes
- Emphasis on readability and visual hierarchy
- Seamless dark/light mode transitions

The design prioritizes flexibility, allowing granular customization while maintaining a cohesive visual language across different interface components.

   - ✅ **OKLCH color system** with semantic tokens

   - ✅ **Professional buttons** with interaction states
   - ✅ **Enhanced search overlay** with backdrop blur

### **Quality Improvements:**
- **Performance**: Optimized CSS with proper layering

- **Consistency**: Unified design tokens across all components

### **Current Status:**
